function planString( items ) {
	var index = 0, message = "", msg = "", item;
	for ( index = 0 ; index < items.length; index++ ){
			item = items[ index ];
			msg = "\t\"name\"\t: \"스벅_"+shopName[index] +"\",\n";
			
			if ( item["name"] ){
				console.log("\"name\" : \"" + item["name"] + "\"" );
				msg += "\t\"jname\"\t: \""+ item["name"] + "\",\n";
			}
			msg += "\t\"code\"\t: \"starbucks_"+item.id +"\",\n";
			if ( item["latlng"] ) {
				msg += "\t\"lat\"\t: \""+ ( parseInt ( item["latlng"].Latitude  * 1000000 ) / 1000000 )+"\",\n";
				msg += "\t\"lng\"\t: \""+( parseInt (item["latlng"].Longitude  * 1000000 ) / 1000000 )+"\",\n";
			}
			if (  item["url"] ) {
				msg += "\t\"b_url\"\t: \"http://www.starbucks.co.jp/"+item["url"]+"\",\n";

			}
			msg += "\t\"icon\"\t: \"coffee\",\n";
			msg += "\t\"ctg\"\t: \"ctg_sapporo\",\n";
			msg += "\t\"maker\"\t: true\n";
			message += "{\n" +msg + "}, "
	}
	return message;
}
